border="0"><tbody><tr><td><div style="overflow:hidden"><font size="-1"><div dir="ltr"><div>Put your hand down and <i>carry on</i> if you think it would be easier and more effective to just nationalize the press.</div><div><blockquote style="margin:0px 0px 0px 40px;border:none;padding:0px"><div><br></div><div>I want to blame you getting two emails today on my gmail scheduler, the &quot;fire&quot; was supposed to get sent early this morning; so it would be fresh in your minds on Monday morning for you to write an article, or a memo to your boss, or a colleague.   Instead i&#39;ll mention that the spark in that e-mail is designed to help you change the world--to do the stuff you want, to really make a change.  To break your company in half, or install a dictator of the Universe... if that&#39;s <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=645460&amp;l=89518338-b2f6-4572-b1e0-b83bc27a7f9f&amp;r=91b65737-8a1b-4fa7-b0af-1379077c6359" target="_blank" style="text-decoration-line:none">what you vote for.</a>  For that link, I will remind you that I am very sure that the historical representations of the Anti-Christ (<a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=645460&amp;l=fb2e7ede-a1ca-4230-b847-dbbb25b4583e&amp;r=91b65737-8a1b-4fa7-b0af-1379077c6359" target="_blank" style="text-decoration-line:none">JC</a>, <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=645460&amp;l=22e48c8d-3a66-4896-bef9-f45f363aefb1&amp;r=91b65737-8a1b-4fa7-b0af-1379077c6359" target="_blank" style="text-decoration-line:none">NP</a>, and <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=645460&amp;l=e84304f5-81d7-49fb-b0e1-3715a40cfa32&amp;r=91b65737-8a1b-4fa7-b0af-1379077c6359" target="_blank" style="text-decoration-line:none">AH</a> are tagged verbosely) are a hidden record of previous incarnations of ... my life ... just like you might see the same pattern in the Horsemen of the Apocalypse, and the series of creation God&#39;s of ancient Egypt.. from <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=645460&amp;l=9324e510-f0c3-47fa-b349-e04bf4623463&amp;r=91b65737-8a1b-4fa7-b0af-1379077c6359" target="_blank" style="text-decoration-line:none">Atum</a> to Ra, through <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=645460&amp;l=a75ec5f3-9bff-40d4-a65b-fc3da9640d6f&amp;r=91b65737-8a1b-4fa7-b0af-1379077c6359" target="_blank" style="text-decoration-line:none">St. Peter</a>.</div></blockquote></div><div><br></div>Imagine a world where, like an overnight sensation this story broke on every network.  No need to give anyone credit for taking the leap, and caring about the truth more than the tooth fairy; so single person other than the President is responsible for &quot;finding Jesus Christ.&quot;  Of course, he merely did the unthinkable and used his newly acquired series of defense contractors.. formerly known Lockheed, Northrop Grumman and Martin Marietta to strong arm Area 51 into opening their records of time travel escapades to the new America Illumination Corporation... and then instantly notified the public of <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=645460&amp;l=c501e02e-089b-4961-9905-746e66c1d0e7&amp;r=91b65737-8a1b-4fa7-b0af-1379077c6359" target="_blank" style="text-decoration-line:none">the existence of a Time Lord</a> (UOA) in South Florida... for capture.  Don&#39;t worry, the contract bidding process was taken into account for the decrease in number of bidders--and the results of those deals... an automated army of peacemakers to replace the recently &quot;fired&quot; police force was released under the newly modified &quot;For Our Interests, America&quot; Act. <div><br></div><div>I really am glad we had this opportunity to work together, Donald... please, don&#39;t take it personally.  On social media, something my readers have yet to discover the value of, I&#39;ve commented that this appears to be the start of &quot;America&#39;s <i>Darkest Comedy Hour</i>.&quot;  In a world which I&#39;ve been sure to describe as Satan&#39;s delightful land of highlighting <i>the things that once caused a financial ice age</i>&quot; one of my prime examples has always been the loss of the &quot;for the people&quot; in our government by a campaign contribution policy that literally puts the financial and ... well, basically if a congressperson wants to keep their job, they have to follow corporate interests--something that is diametrically opposed to the &quot;spirit of our great land.&quot;  Anyway, in this place... where these kinds of things are not just being highlighted by forcing &quot;severe extremity&quot; it only makes sense for one of the most well known business men in the world to be elected President... right in the wake of <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=645460&amp;l=fc433ae3-0db0-4ad8-abb6-80e015c5ad4f&amp;r=91b65737-8a1b-4fa7-b0af-1379077c6359" target="_blank" style="text-decoration-line:none">my sermon</a> about <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=645460&amp;l=c1f6d6bc-a15f-4383-b495-21818e08586f&amp;r=91b65737-8a1b-4fa7-b0af-1379077c6359" target="_blank" style="text-decoration-line:none">Congressional term limits</a>.  That website, <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=645460&amp;l=80de1b71-d65b-49d0-979b-8dc86088a90f&amp;r=91b65737-8a1b-4fa7-b0af-1379077c6359" target="_blank" style="text-decoration-line:none">countable.us</a>, of note.. as the kind of thing that might turn into a &quot;real democracy&quot; were there .. you know, more than one of them and people just a little more interested in &quot;commenting&quot; about legislation they care about.<br></div><div><br></div><div><font size="4">Back to the topic at hand, if you happen to be of the opinion that the recent </font><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=645460&amp;l=39937953-a446-45fd-b898-0b1a7f114351&amp;r=91b65737-8a1b-4fa7-b0af-1379077c6359" target="_blank" totalitarian dictatorship... is having a negative impact on not just the <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=645460&amp;l=7a460104-1b83-4400-a9ab-7d81372ce331&amp;r=91b65737-8a1b-4fa7-b0af-1379077c6359" target="_blank" style="text-decoration-line:none">reviews of Ivanka&#39;s book</a></font><font size="4">, </font><i><font size="4" face="times new roman, serif"><b>The Trump Card </b></font></i><span style="font-family:&quot;times new entire process of &quot;continuing freedom&quot; </font><font size="4" style="font-style:italic">not just in America... well, you agree with </font><font size="6" face="times new roman, serif" style="font-style:italic"><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=645460&amp;l=246f8f80-83ef-4ca8-8137-f9bc2da7047e&amp;r=91b65737-8a1b-4fa7-b0af-1379077c6359" target="_blank" time to start talking about using those Anti-Trust laws</b><font size="4"><i>... you know, to protect the interests of the truth and the people  </i>What you see before you is nothing short of the end of democracy, realize that--because this is your last, best hope for <i><font face="times new roman, serif">fixing it.</font></i></font></div><div><br></div><div>I&#39;m not calling you a <b>fool</b>, that&#39;s my Trump Card, really.  I swear, that 0, that&#39;s the sign of the sun--I mean it&#39;s really it&#39;s symbol.  </div><div><br></div><div>Guys, this is a link to a website called &quot;Twitter,&quot; according to God it&#39;s one of the places where you can really easily see that the government--or some force of invisible aliens--has implemented a censor wall... all over our internet.  If you care about that sort of thing, still.  If not, check your head.  Anyway, <i><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=645460&amp;l=968f3167-d1bd-4519-8a62-8e0982af64df&amp;r=91b65737-8a1b-4fa7-b0af-1379077c6359" target="_blank" style="text-decoration-line:none"><b>here&#39;s the link</b> to the Office of Government Ethics suggesting Trump divest his interests to the Vatican</a></i>--that&#39;s like a &quot;mailing address&quot; for sites on the internet--which is a fancy communications tool, one created by the American Military in order to prevent losing communications infrastructure in the event of... oh, sh!t.</div><div><br></div><div>See the <font face="arial black, sans-serif">light</font>, this is <font face="times new roman, serif">not funny.</font></div><div><font face="times new roman, I first have to prove that he exists, and that he is speaking to us, <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=9c038033-91cc-4bc6-a73e-2f3782c1a48b&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="text-decoration-line:none">through our very own hands.</a>  I need your help to do that, I don&#39;t know if this is the right way to attack the problem, but to me... the Bible Code is very clearly a signal hidden within noise--take that from that what you will.<br></div><div><br></div><blockquote style="margin:0px 0px 0px 40px;border:none;padding:0px">I am of the opinion that this is a problem similar to code cracking, to decryption--just as I see language translation.  I am sure that the &quot;Bible Code&quot; is a mathematically solvable problem, just as <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=a24f933f-cb1a-41b4-b198-e5b36faa30ae&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="text-decoration-line:none">the &quot;hidden language</a>&quot; at Isiaah 52:13; which is quite the important verse--for me.  I am sure I found it before in Jeremiah, and Revelation, and Exodus--I bet you find it near the stories of Lazarus and Samson too.  I&#39;m sure it&#39;s in a great many books--and that it probably will be the kind of thing that can be proven to be non-coincidental, non-random to some degree that nobody in their right mind would call something as glaringly obvious of a sign ... &quot;chance&quot; that you see below.  The assassination in Moby Dick--the name Mob-why; and the ridiculously accurate descriptions of murder weapons attached to the names and dates.... it&#39;s something that sickens me that this has been allowed to be called &quot;normal.&quot; I stumble into a <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=418c8fa3-a057-4f85-8ae2-69a941977fea&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;text-decoration-line:none">well spun story</a> designed by the three fates themselves,  The meaning of Christ&#39;s name, El Elyon--one might only ask why.  Setup, and very, very high--echoes Isaiah 52:13 in the seminal premonition of the Second Coming that hands on a sliver platter my given name crossed directly on top of the words &quot;Jesus Christ,&quot; &quot;framed&quot; and &quot;mafia.&quot;  Not so far away, in the magical land of Mary the subcontracted companies responsible for the NSA&#39;s sale of privacy and identity to the Vatican and their not-so-secret global network of subversion; they might wonder aloud how it is that Mary&#39;s name tells me so surely what it is that we fight against--truly--&quot;the enemy&quot; of Almost Famous, it&#39;s corruption and secrecy and believe I know where it&#39;s rooted.  Look to an ancient story, the old fall of Rome to figure out why it is that corruption never &quot;wins the day.&quot;   This will falter, a low of 666 on the S&amp;P we&#39;re already on the way.  then another all time high, haven&#39;t you had enough of <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=a5dd8168-4730-4fb9-8767-766a64cdd3d2&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;text-decoration-line:none">this roller coaster ride</a>?  </font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif"><br></font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif">It&#39;s a microcosmic map of our future--this time line you think is the past.  Do you wonder if we are already in the dark ages, or if it&#39;s about to end?  Oh right, we&#39;re standing firm <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=b280b459-6d64-4af8-bf78-667f4e3c4fc6&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;text-decoration-line:none">at the Fall of Rome</a>--&quot;<a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=a1277901-2080-4d44-b4b7-eb4a3e5b9197&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;text-decoration-line:none">I thought this place was an <b>((Emperor)) </b>now I&#39;m relaxed, I am sure.</a>&quot;</font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif"><br></font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif">P2? &quot;<a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=7a471490-91ff-4768-8807-68d6bedccfed&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;text-decoration-line:none">Could it be you?</a>&quot;  From the East... the secrecy stops here and now.</font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif"><br></font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif">&quot;<a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=e7991f7f-1f27-4b40-8104-5702381a6005&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;text-decoration-line:none">Every town is Babylon</a>,&quot; Live sings with a roar--Adam and Eve right before your eyes, and yet you stumble at the word &quot;hi.&quot;   &quot;<a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=214c3a64-63da-4aed-9048-10d33d8f706b&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;text-decoration-line:none">I&#39;m giving the commodities a rain check</a>,&quot; a little bit bigger than this, I&#39;ll admit.  Why don&#39;t you understand?<br></font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif"><br></font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif">Say Maryland one more time, and just like the land of Clark Kent &quot;you are CK why?&quot; you might begin to see every single day from here forward how God has written a map to Salvation, and plastered it all over the globe.  <i>Salud.</i></font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif"><br></font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif"><i>They</i> own the Police, the courts, and <i>the press too</i>--&quot;<a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=7566cd49-e2ac-4f87-a4f8-e96f42a2df4e&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;text-decoration-line:none">I&#39;ve had enough, we&#39;re not property.... and I am <i>Stronger</i> than yesterday.</a>&quot;  Secrets and lies, there&#39;s your real systemic risk.  I am a glowing sign, everything they do wrong in a neat little package for the future to unwrap.  Light me up, the future is tomorrow.  </font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif"><br></font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif">What a world I&#39;ve been tossed into.  Who are they?  Has anyone ever really seen them?  I haven&#39;t.  Weird little invisible body snatchers... or no?  Is the Lord of Hosts something else?  </font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif"><br></font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif">2014, Charleston South Carolina; I stared up at the sky--well hidden itself by a roof ful of popcorn and three days awake; and it came alive.  The whole ceiling like an LCD display from Sky-net, just like at the ball game--except the pixels were plaster--&quot;Hello Adam&quot; and &quot;wow,&quot; complete with animated special effects, for all of thirty seconds a hallucination, or a delusion, please--this wasn&#39;t trails and a halo around lights... words on the sky from where?</font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif"><br></font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif">The shrinks and the spooks, the blind fools hiding clear communication from the beyond--they&#39;ll learn to listen, I swear.  &quot;<a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=489aa4ab-bdd6-4768-a54c-4ae05cafac05&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;text-decoration-line:none">Lesson for them, not me.</a>&quot;  Rumors insisted?  Taken into custody?  A story written in stone and blood, one designed to bring about a golden renaissance, one I will see with my own eyes. </font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif"><br></font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif">A little over a year earlier--every time I danced into &quot;Morpheus&#39;s rabbit hole&quot; the same face appeared in my chandelier.  He looked like a puppet, this prop, a little like King Friday only holding a magic wand that he waved.  Literally on one of those days I heard Pope Francis exclaim on the radio &quot;God is not magical,&quot; earning a chuckle from me.  </font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif"><br></font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif">You might never hear the stories told to me; at least not here. I&#39;m doing everything I can to give you what you need- a catalyst to wake up and take control.  </font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif"><br></font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif">I&#39;ve shown you science.. chemistry and computers... at the heart of Christianity; and still you fail to see the light--the magic is coming, the show and the steal.  I&#39;m really telling you why, how <i>this</i> lead me down a path where the enemy was sure I&#39;d lost--a life preserved from a den of fools--not seeing themselves lit with spotlights in the sky.</font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif"><br></font></div><div><font face="times new roman, serif">Did you need more light?  More proof?  Another tie between JC and me, or religion and now?  Come on, have a heart... not getting this message spells &quot;the end.&quot;  </font></div><div style="text-align:right"><br></div><div style="text-align:right"><font size="1">The stock ticket &quot;PLOW&quot; was chosen psuedorandomly. </font></div><div style="text-align:right"><font size="1"><br></font></div><h1 class="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-thumbcaption" style="border:none;line-height:1.4em;padding:3px;font-size:12.3704px;text-align:left"><div class="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-magnify" style="float:right;margin-left:3px;margin-right:0px"><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=679f6b32-ed63-424a-a2df-c6d48a83a74c&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" class="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-internal" title="Enlarge" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-color:initial;display:block;text-indent:15px;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;width:15px;height:11px"></a></div><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=fa249861-7356-484d-b468-23cbe183e70a&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Book of Exodus" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">Exodus</a> 1:1-6. Biblia Hebraica from Kittel&#39;s edition (BHK) 1909. Four letters, 50 letters apart, starting from the first <i><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=7726e28a-6cba-444e-a5f2-a879fe3dae26&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Taw" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">taw</a></i> on the first verse, form the word <big>תורה</big> (<i>Torah</i>).</div></div></div><p style="margin:0.5em 0px;line-height:inherit">The <b>Bible code</b> (<a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=3de442d3-2278-4d56-ac89-315e61a56242&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Hebrew language" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">Hebrew</a>: <span lang="he" dir="rtl">הצופן התנ&quot;כי</span>‎‎, <i>hatzofen hatanachi</i>), also known as the <b>Torah code</b>, is a purported set of <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=1ddfed7b-384d-42e9-853a-7caca6d1d2dd&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Cipher" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">secret messages</a> encoded within the Hebrew text of the <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=58232363-aeba-49fa-8076-db17ca34a639&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Torah" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">Torah</a>. This hidden code has been described as a method by which specific letters from the text can be selected to reveal an otherwise obscured message. Although Bible codes have been postulated and studied for centuries, the subject has been popularized in modern times by <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=71ffae7a-f92d-47c5-aedd-a3a002c8dcf4&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Michael Drosnin" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">Michael Drosnin</a>&#39;s book <i><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=25cba7f0-63f2-4637-ad13-8b6208862bdb&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="The Bible Code (book)" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">The Bible Code</a></i> and the movie <i><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=7143e4c4-db36-4898-9301-6a0be3a9a40f&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="The Omega Code" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">The Omega Code</a></i>.</p><p style="margin:0.5em 0px;line-height:inherit">Many examples have been documented in the past. One cited example is that by taking every 50th letter of the <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=089f1807-b2b2-4055-9748-d755613ad34f&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Book of Genesis" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">Book of Genesis</a> starting with the first <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=7726e28a-6cba-444e-a5f2-a879fe3dae26&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Taw" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">taw</a>, the Hebrew word &quot;<a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=58232363-aeba-49fa-8076-db17ca34a639&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Torah" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">torah</a>&quot; is spelled out. The same happens in the <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=fa249861-7356-484d-b468-23cbe183e70a&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Book of Exodus" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">Book of Exodus</a>. Modern computers have been used to search for similar patterns and more complex variants, as well as quantifying its statistical likelihood.</p></div></div><div style="text-align:right"><span style="color:rgb(37,37,37);font-family:sans-serif;font-size:0.875em">Some tests purportedly showing statistically significant codes in the Bible were published as a &quot;challenging puzzle&quot; in a peer-reviewed academic journal in 1994, and later questioned.</span><font size="1"> </font></div><div style="text-align:right"><font size="1"><br></font></div><div><div id="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-contentSub" class="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-firstHeading" style="font-size:1.8em;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial;font-weight:normal;margin:0px 0px 0.25em;overflow:visible;padding:0px;border-bottom:1px solid rgb(170,170,170);line-height:1.3;font-family:&quot;linux libertine&quot;,georgia,times,serif">They didn&#39;t like my additions.  <i>Finish the pattern.</i><br></h1><div id="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-bodyContent" class="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-mw-body-content" style="color:rgb(37,37,37);font-size:0.875em;line-height:1.6"><div id="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-siteSub" style="font-size:12.88px">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div><div id="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-siteSub" style="font-size:12.88px"><span style="font-size:14px">The </span><b style="font-size:14px">Bible code</b><span style="font-size:14px"> (</span><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=3de442d3-2278-4d56-ac89-315e61a56242&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Hebrew language" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-color:initial;font-size:14px;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial">Hebrew</a><span style="font-size:14px">: </span><span lang="he" dir="rtl" style="font-size:14px">צפנים בתנ&quot;ך</span><span style="font-size:14px">‎‎), also known as the </span><b style="font-size:14px">Torah code</b><span style="font-size:14px">, is a purported set of secret messages encoded within the Hebrew text of the </span><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=58232363-aeba-49fa-8076-db17ca34a639&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Torah" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-color:initial;font-size:14px;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial">Torah</a><span style="font-size:14px">. This </span><i style="font-size:14px">hidden code</i><span style="font-size:14px"> has been described as a method by which specific letters from the text can be selected to reveal an otherwise obscured message. Though Bible codes have been postulated and studied for centuries, the subject has been popularized in modern times by Michael Drosnin&#39;s book </span><i style="font-size:14px"><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=25cba7f0-63f2-4637-ad13-8b6208862bdb&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="The Bible Code (book)" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">The Bible Code</a></i><span style="font-size:14px"> and the movie </span><i style="font-size:14px"><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=7143e4c4-db36-4898-9301-6a0be3a9a40f&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="The Omega Code" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">The Omega Code</a></i><span style="font-size:14px">.</span></div></div></div></div><div id="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-mw-content-ltr" style="direction:ltr"><p style="font-family:sans-serif;color:rgb(37,37,37);font-size:14px;margin:0.5em 0px;line-height:inherit">Many examples have been documented in the past. One cited example is that by taking every 49th letter of the <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=089f1807-b2b2-4055-9748-d755613ad34f&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Book of Genesis" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">Book of Genesis</a> starting with the first <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=7726e28a-6cba-444e-a5f2-a879fe3dae26&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Taw" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">taw</a>, the Hebrew word &quot;<a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=58232363-aeba-49fa-8076-db17ca34a639&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Torah" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">torah</a>&quot; is spelled out, the same happens in the <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=fa249861-7356-484d-b468-23cbe183e70a&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Book of Exodus" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">Book of Exodus</a>. The word &quot;<a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=58232363-aeba-49fa-8076-db17ca34a639&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Torah" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">torah</a>&quot; is spelled in reverse order, in the same manner, in the <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=c829808a-9be9-4b74-9782-82e72effb2d7&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Book of Numbers" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">Book of Numbers</a> and the <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=9adeb43e-017d-4353-8d75-76e5d648f00e&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Book of Deuteronomy" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">Book of Deuteronomy</a>. The <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=a436c83d-3b61-4e43-aa44-992794ebe610&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" title="Book of Leviticus" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">Book of Leviticus</a>, contains the <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=e5aedc4e-9524-4958-b674-2e5228a44131&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" class="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-mw-redirect" title="Tetragramatton" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;color:rgb(11,0,128);text-decoration-line:none;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;background-color:initial">Tetragramatton</a> encoded using ELS with a skip of 7, with all four other books pointing towards it. The word Modern computers have been used to search for similar patterns and more complex variants, and published as a &quot;challenging puzzle&quot; in a peer-reviewed academic journal in 1994. Proponents hold that it is exceedingly unlikely such sequences could arise by chance, while skeptics and opponents hold that such sequences do often arise by chance, as demonstrated on other Hebrew and English texts.<sup id="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-cite_ref-1" class="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-reference" style="line-height:1;unicode-bidi:isolate;white-space:nowrap;font-size:11.2px"><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=803914a7-9b36-4794-ae3b-908c41fc7617&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" See the </span><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=4d4d2254-fb56-47ba-9f8c-cea2dda1a212&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="font-family:&quot;times new roman&quot;;color:rgb(37,37,37);text-decoration-line:none;font-size:large">Princess Di</a><span style="font-family:&quot;times new roman&quot;;font-size:large"> page for details.</span><h3 style="font-family:&quot;times new roman&quot;;font-size:14px">A note to the credulous</h3><span style="font-family:&quot;times new roman&quot;;font-size:large">It has come to my attention that some people have taken this page as claiming that Moby Dick </span><b style="font-family:&quot;times new roman&quot;;font-size:large">really predicted</b><span style="font-family:&quot;times new roman&quot;;font-size:large"> the assassinations of famous people. Please be assured that none of these patterns happened by other than pure random chance.</span><p style="font-family:&quot;times new roman&quot;;font-size:large">No laws of probability are violated here, or even stretched a little. <b>That is also true of Drosnin&#39;s book</b>, which is the whole point of this page. Once you learn Drosnin&#39;s rules (none) and the method (a bit of messy programming) you can find things like this anywhere. The reason it looks amazing is that the number of possible things to look for, and the number of places to look, is much greater than you imagine.</p><h1 id="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-firstHeading" class="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-firstHeading" lang="en" style="font-family:&quot;linux libertine&quot;,georgia,times,serif;font-size:1.8em;background-color:initial;background-image:none;background-position:initial;background-size:initial;background-repeat:initial;background-origin:initial;background-clip:initial;font-weight:normal;margin:0px 0px 0.25em;overflow:visible;padding:0px;border-bottom:1px solid rgb(170,170,170);line-height:1.3">Predicting <i><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=2d4b1c0a-a626-4444-9885-e4cd7edd2d21&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;text-decoration-line:none">organized crime</a></i> related assassinations apparently... not the &quot;stuff&quot; of religion?</h1><div><font color="#000000" face="times new roman" size="4"><br></font></div><div><font color="#000000" face="times new roman" size="4">Is now.  Published on 4/27/2013, in <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=03c92f98-7897-4fcf-88d9-ebe0b1a2615e&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="font-family:arial,sans-serif;text-decoration-line:none">Timelike Syncrhonicity</a>, a refutation of Drosnen&#39;s complete idiocy.  </font></div></div><div><font color="#000000" face="times new roman" size="4"><br></font></div><div><div id="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-page-title" style="font-family:purisa,arial,helvetica,sans-serif;margin:0px 0px 0.5em;padding:0px 30px;font-size:xx-large;border-bottom:none;font-weight:bold">Assassination Synchronicity</div><div id="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-page-content" style="font-family:verdana,arial,helvetica,sans-serif;padding:10px 30px;min-height:600px;font-size:13.12px"><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif">Two very public cases do a good job of portraying the broad means by which mind control could be used to coerce or trick someone into being an actual Manchurian Candidate.  <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=85d1f633-80a7-489b-896a-628485095d02&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(251,100,0);text-decoration-line:none">Sirhan Sirhan</a>, the shooter who killed Robert F. Kennedy, apparently believed that he was in a shooting range, and nobody was in any danger.  He believed he was touched by an <em>angel</em>, a strangely beautiful woman, on the shoulder; just before the shooting range hallucination began.  After the assassination, he stood in disbelief, waiting to be apprehended, no attempt was made to escape.  On the far side of the gamut, mind control could be used for an extended period of time to foster a life long delusion.</p><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif"><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=e4e2dafe-5a99-483d-96cc-883f08c3362b&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(251,100,0);text-decoration-line:none">Mark David Chapman</a> believed he was being tempted by the devil, and that he spoke to God.  Just before shooting John Lennon, Chapman saw &quot;Thou Shalt Not Kill&quot; flash on a television screen, manipulation of television programming is a common theme among mind control victims.  These cases might also point you in the right direction of the perpetrator of the crime, or you could look at <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=1a34dfe0-2cff-435e-8386-53af90cfe728&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(251,100,0);text-decoration-line:none">John Hinkley Jr.</a> and <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=d2b3069e-7b3c-4979-9e3c-d0a3b483d93d&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(251,100,0);text-decoration-line:none">Lee Harvey Oswald</a>, but <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=367fc1f3-646f-42af-83e3-39939e0b3b25&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(251,100,0);text-decoration-line:none">I&#39;m</a><em><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=367fc1f3-646f-42af-83e3-39939e0b3b25&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(251,100,0);text-decoration-line:none"> not sure how</a> you could <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=07f97876-d4c7-4965-98bd-0ae5744b1bcf&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(251,100,0);text-decoration-line:none">link those together</a>.</em></p><h2 id="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-toc0" style="font-family:purisa,arial,helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:19.68px">The Pattern</h2><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif"><strong><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=2f32b99e-bfc4-4bb9-bd71-c69663b7525c&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(251,100,0);text-decoration-line:none">Timelike Synchronicity</a></strong> is the <em>fingerprint</em> of a monolithic entity behind  the <em>prophetic</em> authoring of <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=99e19527-b781-43b9-8322-7693087265c6&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(251,100,0);text-decoration-line:none">1984 and Brave New World</a>, a pattern which manifests in the cases of several assassins who have been linked to <em>a</em> mind control conspiracy.  This pattern is noted by equidistant spans of years between <em>pivotal events topically pertinent to the microcosmic pattern</em>.  Sirhan Sirhan, in a parallel to Orwell and Huxley&#39;s entry to Eton (Eden), had <strong>12</strong> years pass between his birth in <em>Jerusalem</em> and his entry to the United States of America.  Exactly <strong>12</strong> years later he assassinated Robert F. Kennedy in <strong>1968</strong>.  This same year is the midpoint between John Hinkley Jr,&#39;s birth, and the attempted assassination of Ronald Reagan.  Exactly <strong>12</strong> years later, in 1980, Mark David Chapman assassinated John Lennon, the midpoint between his birth, and the Reagan assassination attempt was also <strong>1968</strong>.  This year also happens to be the midpoint of the arrest and <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=367fc1f3-646f-42af-83e3-39939e0b3b25&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(251,100,0);text-decoration-line:none">trial of Clay L. Shaw</a>, as well as the midpoint between the assassination of JFK, and the suspicious death of Shaw.</p><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif">Ironically, or perhaps telling, Lee Harvey Oswald has no noticeable synchronicity.</p><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif">Martin Luther King, assassinated in <strong>1968</strong>, with implications of COINTELPRO and government involvement entered seminary in <strong>1948,</strong>the midpoint between his birth and death; and also the year <strong>1984</strong> was written.  Incidentally 1984 began on the day of King&#39;s assassination, April 4.</p><table style="font-size:10.496px;text-align:center;font-style:italic"></td></tr></tbody></table><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif">Non coincidentally, this pattern of equidistant periods has also been revealed in the <strong><a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=577a0153-143b-445d-b950-3095e5bf7117&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" A number of assassinations, overlapping significantly with the group above, were <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=0c08c38d-77a5-45d8-a677-c3fa493b2b3c&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(251,100,0);text-decoration-line:none">decoded within the text of Moby Dick</a>, written over a hundred years before they occurred.</p><h2 id="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-toc1" style="font-family:purisa,arial,helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:19.68px">It&#39;s not <em>just</em> the assassins.</h2><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif">While the ability to "remotely control" a human being is without doubt within the capabilities of intelligence organizations such as the Central Intelligence Agency, MI-6, and the former KGB, remote neural stimulation <em>could also be </em>much more subtle. It could be used to make you ignore, or not care about something that you would otherwise find important, like <em>democracy, privacy,</em> and <em>f<wbr>reedom of speech</em>. It could make you believe that something you read which you would otherwise find <em>intelligent and thought provoking</em> is.. <em>off the wall</em>. Mind control could be used to make you forgive a person or an organization, maybe your <em>government</em> for something that you probably shouldn&#39;t forgive them for. It is possible that it would be so subtle that you would never, ever know it was happening to you.  Much like Mark David Chapman, many could be made to blame &quot;inner demons&quot; for their actions, despite resounding evidence to the contrary.  </p><blockquote style="border:1px dashed rgb(153,153,153);padding:0px 1em;background-color:rgb(244,244,244)"><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif">I saw a star that had fallen from the sky to the earth. The star was given the <strong>key to the shaft of the Abyss</strong>.  </p><blockquote style="border:1px dashed rgb(153,153,153);padding:0px 1em"><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif">-Revelation 9:1</p></blockquote></blockquote><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif">In the late 1940&#39;s, two monumental events, whose origin is decidedly unearthly, shaped the future of America and the world.  The whole of America was gripped with reported sightings of flying saucers, epitomized by the RAAF cover up of a UFO crash in Roswell, NM.  At the very same time, the CIA began researching <strong>mind control</strong>, these experiments would coincide temporally with the phenomenon of alien contact.</p><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif">Had an alien craft been recovered, what kind of technology would be on board?  Perhaps these two things are liked by more than time, but rather the UFO phenomenon was the very source of the mind control technology — a technology which evolved so rapidly between 1948 and 1963 that it certainly appears that it was being reverse engineered, rather than developed from scratch.  </p><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif">For working technology to have been developed by the time of the congressional hearings on the subjects, with enough time for a significant number of records to have been destroyed prior to the end of the hearings, it is almost undeniable that it had to be <em>given</em> to the CIA.  So far ahead of modern neuroscience would the Agency have had to have been, that it would have been <em>impossible</em> for them to have not used public research, leaking significant advances in knowledge of neural function that did not occur.</p><h2 id="gmail-m_-1195406827001876965m_4977814675551871484m_1910056946444932447m_-2761396498300659420m_-7450255576899686946gmail-m_7212919974513149311gmail-m_2974993816985132450gmail-m_313305242438984565gmail-m_-3417769882202642932gmail-toc2" style="font-family:purisa,arial,helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:19.68px">What does it all mean?</h2><blockquote style="border:1px dashed rgb(153,153,153);padding:0px 1em;background-color:rgb(244,244,244)"><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif">The dragon gave the beast his <strong>power</strong> and his throne and <strong>great authority</strong>. </p><blockquote style="border:1px dashed rgb(153,153,153);padding:0px 1em"><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif">-Revelation 13:2</p></blockquote></blockquote><p style="font-family:arial,sans-serif">This is one example of the influence of an intelligent force over assassinations. There are <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=0c08c38d-77a5-45d8-a677-c3fa493b2b3c&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(251,100,0);text-decoration-line:none">others</a>, clearly it wants us to know. These assassinations, and their popular culture relation to <em>mind control</em>, and the MK-ULTRA program add a piece to the puzzle of <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=45db6cad-5040-437e-a438-7b7178186154&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(251,100,0);text-decoration-line:none">The Octopus</a>. Like the delivery of the prescient messages in the <a href="http://whoiscoming.reallyhim.com/x/c?c=664900&amp;l=6bcd08f3-1091-437e-899a-b3ef449a78d3&amp;r=1f4ec4ae-2f77-4963-ad39-9963468c6f06" target="_blank" style="color:rgb(251,100,0);text-decoration-line:none">Dystopic and apocalyptic works</a>, there is nearly no other alternative explanation for its very existence other than a technology which can manipulate the thoughts and actions of humans… without them knowing.</p></div></div><div><font color="#000000" face="times new roman"><font size="4">/s/  Jesus </font><i><font size="6">f</font></i><font size="4">.
